      "title": "How Layers Of Buildup Are Removed From Hardwood Floors | Art Insider",
      "description": "Truman's Hardwood Floor Refinishing & Cleaning specializes in removing wax buildup from hardwood floors. Courtney Lee explains that this wax comes from an owner's DIY attempts to polish, protect, or refinish their floors using products they find in a hardware store that claim to revitalize flooring. The issue is that this wax sits on top of the wood instead of soaking into it. The wax will soften over time and bond to dirt and hold it there, which can make the wood dirty and change its color. It's nearly impossible to refinish the floor by sanding it, since the layers of wax are often thick and piled on.\n\nFor more, visit:\nwww.trumanhardwoodrefinishing.com\nhttps://www.facebook.com/TrumanSteemerscarpetcleaning/\nhttps://youtube.com/c/TrumansHardwoodFloorRefinishingCleaning\n\nMore Art Insider Videos: \nHow Realistic Mermaid Tails Are Made | Art Insider\nhttps://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LDT-rtPMPSk\nPainting Translucent Artwork With Acrylic Paint And Sand | Art Insider\nhttps://youtu.be/xmVU99Sdh0U\nWedding-Venue Designer Restores A Bank's 114 Year Old Floor Tiles | Art Insider\nhttps://youtu.be/5Yb9KiFgXuY\n\n------------------------------------------------------\n#Hardwoodflooring #Cleaning #ArtInsider \n\nInsider is great journalism about what passionate people actually want to know.       "title": "Dip Instantly Turns Jewelry Black",
      "description": "Oxidation is a process in which elements lose electrons. When this happens to metals, their color tarnishes, resulting in a visible change. Common jewelry metals like copper and silver will oxidize, but copper is quicker to do so. By chemically oxidizing the metal in a liver of sulfur bath, jewelers force this color-changing process to happen on their terms. The process can transform both copper and silver from their original hues to nearly black.       "title": "Carboxytherapy Helps Treat Dark Under-Eyes",
      "description": "Carboxytherapy is a nonsurgical treatment where carbon dioxide is injected into the skin to improve circulation, blood flow, and elasticity. The treatment can be done on the scalp, eyes, neck, tummy, legs, and hands. The gas is pumped into the skin through a very fine needle. Clients might briefly feel a cold sensation and tightness, and risks include minimal bruising and swelling at the injection site.       "title": "Eyebrow Transplants Restore Brows With Real Hair",
      "description": "An eyebrow transplant is a permanent way to restore eyebrows with one's natural hair. This treatment can be done on the entire eyebrow or to fill in a just portion of an eyebrow. Beauty Insider visits Natalie Attenello, a double board-certified facial plastic surgeon in Beverly Hills, to see how she performs an eyebrow transplant. The first step is to mark the eyebrows to the desired shape. Then Attenello needs to obtain a strip of hair from a different body part, usually the back of the scalp, to relocate it to the eyebrow area. She separates the hair follicles and individually inserts them into the eyebrows at the correct angle and direction for the hair to grow. It takes about 200 to 300 individual follicles per eyebrow for a full transformation. Although the results are immediate, the transplanted hairs will fall out after a couple weeks, and new hair growth will start in about three months. The procedure usually ranges from $8,000 to $10,000 but can be more depending on the number of follicles needed.
